    svn web管理之submin

    devops svn
    创建时间:2016-12-01 15:54

    svn web管理

    Submin-----SVN、git web administration

1 下载

[https://supermind.nl/submin/current/](https://supermind.nl/submin/current/)

Software&nbsp;Notes

Apache and/or Nginx&nbsp;Submin can generate config files for both. Apache is mandatory for subversion.

Python 2.x&nbsp;Python 2.7 preferred, but 2.6 should work

Subversion&nbsp;Only if you want to use subversion

Git&nbsp;Only if you want to use git

2 配置

&nbsp;关闭防火墙

#停止firewall

&nbsp;#禁止firewall开机启动

systemctl stop firewalld.service

systemctl disable firewalld.service

关闭selinux

setenforce 0

echo &quot;setenforce 0&quot; &gt;&gt; /etc/rc.local

sed -i &#39;s/SELINUX=enforcing/SELINUX=disabled/g&#39;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; /etc/sysconfig/selinux

安装subversion

测试用的是

yum install subversion -y

查看版本

svnserve --version

配置SVN

useradd svn

1)建立目录

# mkdir -p /data/svn

2)建立仓库

# svnadmin create /data/svn/svnrepos

# chown -R svn:svn /data/svn

#chmod -R 770 /data/svn

# ll /data/svn/svnrepos

启动SVN服务

不要以系统自带的service启动

&nbsp;&nbsp; 以svn用户启动

# su - svn -c &quot;svnserve -d -r /data/svn/svnrepos&quot;

检查启动状态

# netstat -tunlp | grep svn

加入开机启动

vim /etc/rc.d/rc.local

添加

# su - svn -c &quot;svnserve -d -r /data/svn/svnrepos&quot;

submin2默认需要sqlite3做数据库

在线安装

yum install sqlite sqlite-devel -y

yum install apr apr-util&nbsp; apr-devel apr-util-devel -y

&nbsp;再安装

yum -y install apr-util-sqlite sqlite-devel mod_dav_svn subversion-python uwsgi mod_wsgi

&nbsp;系统要发邮件

yum remove sendmail -y

yum install postfix&nbsp; -y

&nbsp;/etc/init.d/postfix restart

systemctl start postfix

安装apache/nginx

检查apache是否安装&nbsp;

rpm -qa|grep httpd

使用yum安装apache

yum -y install httpd httpd-devel

&nbsp;要注意httpd版本

centos6：2.2.15

centos7：2.4.6

启动apache测试apache是否可用

service httpd start

注意：在centos7中使用systemctl替换了service

systemctl start httpd.service

systemctl status httpd.service

apache安装路径/etc/httpd

安装submin

tar -zxvf /opt/submin-2.2.2-1.tar.gz -C /opt/

cd /opt/submin-2.2.2-1/

python setup.py install

验证安装

执行 submin2-admin 成功显示当前版本

#&nbsp; submin2-admin

Submin 2.2.2

Usage: /usr/bin/submin2-admin &lt;/path/to/projenv&gt; [command [subcommand] [option]]

配置submin

submin2-admin /opt/submin/ initenv [your@email.address](mailto:your@email.address)

邮箱很重要， submin会将管理员设置初始口令的链接发到这邮箱中

/opt/submin这个目录不要提前建，安装命令的向导一步步设置就可以了，说明很清楚.

这一步需要注意

&nbsp;

####

Submin can enable features for you automatically. Please answer which features

you want to enable. You can choose to enable: &#39;svn&#39;, &#39;git&#39;, &#39;trac&#39;, &#39;apache&#39;

and &#39;nginx&#39;.

Which features do you want to enable? [svn, git, apache, nginx]&gt; 回车

Please provide a location for the Subversion repositories. For new Subversion

repositories, the default setting is ok. If the path is not absolute, it will

be relative to the submin environment. If you want to use an existing

repository, please provide the full pathname to the Subversion parent

directory (ie. /var/lib/svn).

Path to the repository? [svn]&gt; /data/svn/svnrepos

Please provide a location for the git repositories. For new git repositories,

the default setting is ok. If the path is not absolute, it will be relative to

the submin environment. If you want to use an existing repository, please

provide the full pathname to the git parent directory (ie. /var/lib/git).

Path to the git repositories? [git]&gt; 回车

Please provide a hostname that can be used to reach the web interface. This

hostname will be used in communication to the user (a link in email, links

in the web interface). The hostname should be a FQDN, so instead of &#39;foo&#39; it

should be &#39;foo.example.com&#39;. Please correct if the default is incorrect.

Hostname? [localhost.localdomain]&gt; 192.168.184.36

The HTTP path tells Submin where the website is located relative to the root.

This is needed for proper working of the website. Submin will be accesible

from &lt;http base&gt;/submin, Subversion will be accessible from &lt;http base&gt;/svn.

If you use Trac, it will be accessible from &lt;http base&gt;/trac.

HTTP base? [/]&gt; 回车

Submin will send emails for password resets and for commit message (if

enabled). You can set the sender email address that Submin will use. The

default might work in some places, but not all.

Email from envelope? [Submin &lt;[root@localhost.localdomain](mailto:root@localhost.localdomain)&gt;]&gt; Submin &lt;[root@192.168.184.36](mailto:root@192.168.184.36)&gt;

Apache files created:

/opt/submin/conf/apache-webui-cgi.conf

/opt/submin/conf/apache-webui-wsgi.conf

/opt/submin/conf/apache-svn.conf

/opt/submin/conf/apache-trac-modpython.conf

/opt/submin/conf/apache-trac-cgi.conf

/opt/submin/conf/apache-trac-modwsgi.conf

/opt/submin/conf/apache-trac-fcgid.conf

/opt/submin/conf/apache-trac-no-anonymous.conf

/opt/submin/conf/apache-2.4-webui-cgi.conf

/opt/submin/conf/apache-2.4-webui-wsgi.conf

/opt/submin/conf/apache-2.4-svn.conf

/opt/submin/conf/apache-2.4-trac-modpython.conf

/opt/submin/conf/apache-2.4-trac-cgi.conf

/opt/submin/conf/apache-2.4-trac-modwsgi.conf

/opt/submin/conf/apache-2.4-trac-fcgid.conf

/opt/submin/conf/apache-2.4-trac-no-anonymous.conf

&nbsp;&nbsp; Please include ONE of the -webui- files and optionally -trac- and -svn-

&nbsp;&nbsp; files (if you need/want that functionality). The -trac-no-anonymous.conf

&nbsp;&nbsp; file can be used together with ONE other trac config file. The -2.4- files

&nbsp;&nbsp; are for apache &gt;= 2.4.

&nbsp;&nbsp; Hint: cgi is simpler, but performs worse.

&nbsp;&nbsp; Please read the instructions in the file for caveats and on how to include!

Nginx files created:

/opt/submin/conf/nginx-webui-wsgi.conf

/opt/submin/conf/nginx-webui-uwsgi.ini

&nbsp;&nbsp; Please include the&nbsp; relevent .conf files in your NGINX config.

<span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);">经过查看nginx-webui-uwsgi.ini发现submin 用apache用户，用nginx就要注意了</span>

####

配置apache

centos6：

cp /opt/submin/conf/apache-webui-cgi.conf /etc/httpd/conf.d/

cp /opt/submin/conf/apache-svn.conf /etc/httpd/conf.d/

centos7：

cp /opt/submin/conf/apache-2.4-webui-cgi.conf /etc/httpd/conf.d/

cp /opt/submin/conf/apache-2.4-svn.conf /etc/httpd/conf.d/

&nbsp;

vi /etc/httpd/conf/httpd.conf

添加

LoadModule dbd_module&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; modules/mod_dbd.so

LoadModule authn_dbd_module&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; modules/mod_authn_dbd.so

#LoadModule wsgi_module&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; modules/mod_wsgi.so

#LoadModule dav_fs_module&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; modules/mod_dav_fs.so

#LoadModule dav_module&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; modules/mod_dav.so

#LoadModule dav_svn_module&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; modules/mod_dav_svn.so

#LoadModule authz_svn_module&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; modules/mod_authz_svn.so

###

chown -R apache&nbsp;&nbsp; /etc/httpd/

chown -R apache&nbsp;&nbsp; /opt/submin/

chown -R apache&nbsp; /data/svn/svnrepos

重启apache

service httpd restart

systemctl restart httpd.service

暂时不用git--要禁用git

submin2-admin /opt/submin config set vcs_plugins svn

（启用git----&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; submin2-admin /opt/submin git init）

（禁用svn&nbsp;&nbsp; ---submin2-admin /opt/submin config set vcs_plugins git）

###

诊断submin 检查一下

执行以下命令

submin2-admin /opt/submin/ diagnostics

如果有问题参照说明修改对应错误
